UNIVERSITY CALENDAR FOR THE UNDERGRADUATE SCHOOL 
FOR THE YEAR 1949 
Second Semester 
Feb. 1, 2(Tues,, Wed.)....................................................Registration with the Director of Student Accounts and with the Deansfor courses inthe second semester. 
Feb. ^ (Thurs.)................................................................... Classes begin at 8:00 a.m. 
Feb. 5(Sat.) .................................................................. Latest date for change in regis­tration. 
Feb. 22 (Tues.)................................................................... Washington's Birthday.(No classes.) 
March 18 (Fri.)..................................................................Midsemester report of deficient students. 
April 1 ............................................................................Latest datefor submittingentries in contestsfor medals andother prizes. 
Apr. 4to 11 (Mon. to Mon.).............................................Preregistrationincoursesforthefirst semester of 1949-50 and fortheSummerSession of 1949. 
April 13(Wed.)................................................................Easter vacation begins at noon. 
April 20 (Wed.).................................................................Classes resumed at 8:00 a. m. 
April 21 (Thurs.)...........................................................Latest date for comprehensiveexaminations, anddissertations of undergraduates. 
May 26 (Th urs.).................................................................. Feast of the Ascension. (Noclasses.) 
May 27 to June 4 (Fri. to Sat.) Semester examinations for all students. 
May 30 (M on .)............................................................... Memorial Day. 
June 4 (Sat.) ............................................................... Class-day exercises. 
June 5(Sun.) ...............................................................Commencement Mass and bacca­laureate sermom Conferring of degrees at 4:00 p.m. 


CALENDAR FOR THE SUMMER SESSION OF 1949 June 20-21 (Mon.-Tues.) . . . . . . Registration for courses. (No
late registration.) June 22 (Wed.)..........................................................................Classes begin at 8:00 a. m. June 26 (Sun.)................................................................Formal opening of the session 
with Solemn Mass. 

July4 (M on .)................................................................Independence Day. (No classes.) Aug. 5-6 (F ri.-Sat.)................................................ Examinations for seniors. Aug. 11-12 (Thurs.-Fri.)........................................ Examinations in all classes. 
Aug. 12 (F ri.)................................................................Conferringofdegrees,WashingtonHall, 8:00 p.m. 

Registration for classes for the fall semester of 1949-50 will be held September 12, 13 and 14. 
CODES 
CODES AND ABBREVIATIONS 
Explanationofthe codewhichfollows the student’s name inparentheses 


The letter andnumbers whichfollow each student’s name in parentheses are tobe indicated accordingtothefollowingcode. The letter designatesthe college, andthenumbers designate respectivelythe class, semesterandstatus; e.g.,Smith,JohnJ.,(E121) indicatesEngineering, freshman, second semester, civilian.
